# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3`

# Task: Implement CompactDiffFormatter for Terraform

## Objective
Create a `CompactDiffFormatter` in `internal/command/format/` that produces a condensed,
summary-style diff output for `terraform plan`, showing only resource-level changes
without attribute-level detail.

## Requirements

1. **Create `internal/command/format/compact.go`** with:
   - `CompactDiffFormatter` struct implementing a plan formatter
   - `Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *terraform.Schemas)` method returning string
   - Outputs one line per resource change: `[action] resource_type.name`
   - Groups changes by action type (create/update/delete/replace)
   - Shows summary counts at the end

2. **Create `internal/command/format/compact_test.go`** with tests

3. **Follow Terraform patterns**:
   - Study the existing `DiffFormatter` in the format package
   - Use `plans.Action` constants (Create, Update, Delete, etc.)
   - Use `addrs.AbsResourceInstance` for resource addressing

## Key Reference Files
- `internal/command/format/diff.go` — existing diff formatter
- `internal/command/format/state.go` — state formatter pattern
- `internal/plans/changes.go` — plan change types
- `internal/plans/plan.go` — Plan struct definition
- `internal/addrs/resource.go` — resource addressing

## Success Criteria
- CompactDiffFormatter struct exists in format package
- Format method accepts plan and schemas parameters
- Outputs resource-level change summary
- Groups by action type
- Test file exists

     1→// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.
     2→// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1
     3→
     4→package format
     5→
     6→import (
     7→	"bytes"
     8→	"fmt"
     9→	"sort"
    10→
    11→	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs"
    12→	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
    13→	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo"
    14→)
    15→
    16→// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output for
    17→// terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without attribute-level
    18→// detail.
    19→type CompactDiffFormatter struct{}
    20→
    21→// Format returns a compact summary of planned changes grouped by action type.
    22→// Each resource change is shown as a single line with its action and address.
    23→func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {
    24→	if plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {
    25→		return ""
    26→	}
    27→
    28→	// Group resources by action
    29→	actionGroups := make(map[plans.Action][]string)
    30→
    31→	// Collect all resource changes
    32→	for _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {
    33→		// Skip deposed resources
    34→		if rc.DeposedKey != "" {
    35→			continue
    36→		}
    37→
    38→		action := rc.Action
    39→		addr := rc.Addr.String()
    40→		actionGroups[action] = append(actionGroups[action], addr)
    41→	}
    42→
    43→	// Sort addresses within each action group for consistent output
    44→	for _, addresses := range actionGroups {
    45→		sort.Strings(addresses)
    46→	}
    47→
    48→	// Define the order of actions for display
    49→	actionOrder := []plans.Action{
    50→		plans.Create,
    51→		plans.Update,
    52→		plans.Delete,
    53→		plans.DeleteThenCreate,
    54→		pl
... (truncated)

98-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've successfully implemented the `CompactDiffFormatter` for Terraform. Let me create a summary of what was delivered:

## Summary

I've created two files in the `internal/command/format/` directory:

### 1. **compact.go** - The CompactDiffFormatter Implementation

This file contains:
- **CompactDiffFormatter struct**: A formatter that produces condensed, summary-style diff output
- **Format() method**: Main public method accepting `*plans.Plan` and `*schemarepo.Schemas`, returning a formatted string
- **Helper functions**:
  - `actionSymbol()`: Returns symbol representation for each action (+, ~, -, ±, ∓, <=, etc.)
  - `actionToString()`: Returns human-readable names (Create, Update, Delete, Replace, etc.)
  - `summarizeCounts()`: Generates summary line with counts of each action type

**Key features**:
- Groups resource changes by action type (Create, Update, Delete, Replace, etc.)
- Displays changes in a defined order for consistency
- Sorts resource addresses alphabetically within each group
- Skips deposed resources
- Shows summary counts (e.g., "Plan: 1 to create, 2 to update...")
- Handles edge cases (nil plans, empty plans)

### 2. **compact_test.go** - Comprehensive Test Suite

Includes four test functions:
1. **TestCompactDiffFormatter_Format**: Tests the main formatting logic with:
   - Nil plan handling
   - Empty plan handling
   - Single create operation
   - Multiple mixed changes
   - Replace actions
   - Deposed resource filtering

2. **TestCompactDiffFormatter_ActionSymbol**: Tests symbol generation for all action types

3. **TestCompactDiffFormatter_ActionToString**: Tests string conversion for all action types

4. **TestCompactDiffFormatter_SummarizeCounts**: Tests summary count generation with various combinations

## Design Details

The described changes\n25: // are not applied directly, but contain an approximation of the final\n26: // result that will be completed during apply by resolving any values that\n27: // cannot be predicted.\n28: //\n29: // A plan must always be accompanied by the configuration it was built from,\n30: // since the plan does not itself include all of the information required to\n31: // make the changes indicated.\n32: type Plan struct {\n33: \t// Mode is the mode under which this plan was created.\n34: \t//\n35: \t// This is only recorded to allow for UI differences when presenting plans\n36: \t// to the end-user, and so it must not be used to influence apply-time\n37: \t// behavior.   "new_string": "// summarizeCounts returns a summary line with counts of each action type\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) summarizeCounts(groups map[plans.Action][]string) string {\n\tcreates := len(groups[plans.Create])\n\tupdates := len(groups[plans.Update])\n\tdeletes := len(groups[plans.Delete])\n\treplacements := len(groups[plans.DeleteThenCreate]) + len(groups[plans.CreateThenDelete])\n\n\tvar counts []string\n\tif creates > 0 {\n\t\tcounts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to create\", creates))\n\t}\n\tif updates > 0 {\n\t\tcounts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to update\", updates))\n\t}\n\tif deletes > 0 {\n\t\tcounts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to delete\", deletes))\n\t}\n\tif replacements > 0 {\n\t\tcounts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to replace\", replacements))\n\t}\n\n\tif len(counts) == 0 {\n\t\treturn \"Plan: No changes.\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Join counts with commas when multiple\n\tif len(counts) == 1 {\n\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"Plan: %s.\", counts[0])\n\t}\n\n\tcountStr := \"\"\n\tfor i, count := range counts {\n\t\tif i > 0 && i == len(counts)-1 {\n\t\t\tcountStr += \", \" + count\n\t\t} else if i > 0 {\n\t\t\tcountStr += \", \" + count\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tcountStr = count\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"Plan: %s.\", countStr)\n}",

(\n\t\"bytes\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sort\"\n\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo\"\n)\n\n// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output for\n// terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without attribute-level\n// detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format returns a compact summary of planned changes grouped by action type.\n// Each resource change is shown as a single line with its action and address.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Group resources by action\n\tactionGroups := make(map[plans.Action][]string)\n\n\t// Collect all resource changes\n\tfor _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\t// Skip deposed resources\n\t\tif rc.DeposedKey != \"\" {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\taction := rc.Action\n\t\taddr := rc.Addr.String()\n\t\tactionGroups[action] = append(actionGroups[action], addr)\n\t}\n\n\t// Sort addresses within each action group for consistent output\n\tfor _, addresses := range actionGroups {\n\t\tsort.Strings(addresses)\n\t}\n\n\t// Define the order of actions for display\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.NoOp,\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\n\t// Write resources grouped by action in the defined order\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\taddresses, ok := actionGroups[action]\n\t\tif !ok || len(addresses) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Write action header\n\t\tfmt.Fprintf(&buf, \"# %s\\n\", actionToString(action))\n\n\t\t// Write each resource\n\t\tfor _, addr := range addresses {\n\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(&buf, \"%s %s\\n\", actionSymbol(action), addr)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Write summary counts\n\tsummary := f.summarizeCounts(actionGroups)\n\tif summary != \"\" {\n\t\tfmt.Fprintf(&buf, \"%s\\n\", summary)\n\t}\n\n\treturn buf.String()\n}\n\n// actionSymbol returns a short symbol representation of an action\nfunc actionSymbol(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"+\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"~\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"-\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"\u00b1\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"\u2213\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"<=\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \".\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"\u00b1\"\n\tcase plans.NoOp:\n\t\treturn \" \"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"?\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// actionToString returns a human-readable string for an action\nfunc actionToString(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"Create\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"Update\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"Delete\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"Replace\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"Replace\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"Read\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \"Forget\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"Create and Forget\"\n\tcase plans.NoOp:\n\t\treturn \"No-op\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"Unknown\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// summarizeCounts returns a 1. WRITE /workspace/internal/command/format/compact.go
// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.
// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1

package format

import (
	"bytes"
	"fmt"
	"sort"

	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo"
)

// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output for
// terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without attribute-level
// detail.
type CompactDiffFormatter struct{}

// Format returns a compact summary of planned changes grouped by action type.
// Each resource change is shown as a single line with its action and address.
func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {
	if plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {
		return ""
	}

	// Group resources by action
	actionGroups := make(map[plans.Action][]string)

	// Collect all resource changes
	for _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {
		// Skip deposed resources
		if rc.DeposedKey != "" {
			continue
		}

		action := rc.Action
		addr := rc.Addr.String()
		actionGroups[action] = append(actionGroups[action], addr)
	}

	// Sort addresses within each action group for consistent output
	for _, addresses := range actionGroups {
		sort.Strings(addresses)
	}

	// Define the order of actions for display
	actionOrder := []plans.Action{
		plans.Create,
		plans.Update,
		plans.Delete,
		plans.DeleteThenCreate,
		plans.CreateThenDelete,
		plans.Read,
		plans.CreateThenForget,
		plans.Forget,
		plans.NoOp,
	}

	var buf bytes.Buffer

	// Write resources grouped by action in the defined order
	for _, action := range actionOrder {
		addresses, ok := actionGroups[action]
		if !ok || len(addresses) == 0 {
			continue
		}

		// Write action header
		fmt.Fprintf(&buf, "# %s\n", actionToString(a
... (truncated)

3. EDIT /workspace/internal/command/format/compact.go
Before
// summarizeCounts returns a summary line with counts of each action type
func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) summarizeCounts(groups map[plans.Action][]string) string {
	creates := len(groups[plans.Create])
	updates := len(groups[plans.Update])
	deletes := len(groups[plans.Delete])
	replacements := len(groups[plans.DeleteThenCreate]) + len(groups[plans.CreateThenDelete])

	var counts []string
	if creates > 0 {
		counts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to create", creates))
	}
	if updates > 0 {
		counts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to update", updates))
	}
	if deletes > 0 {
		counts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to delete", deletes))
	}
	if replacements > 0 {
		counts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to replace", replacements))
	}

	if len(counts) == 0 {
		return "Plan: No changes."
	}

	return fmt.Sprintf("Plan: %s.", counts)
}
After
// summarizeCounts returns a summary line with counts of each action type
func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) summarizeCounts(groups map[plans.Action][]string) string {
	creates := len(groups[plans.Create])
	updates := len(groups[plans.Update])
	deletes := len(groups[plans.Delete])
	replacements := len(groups[plans.DeleteThenCreate]) + len(groups[plans.CreateThenDelete])

	var counts []string
	if creates > 0 {
		counts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to create", creates))
	}
	if updates > 0 {
		counts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to update", updates))
	}
	if deletes > 0 {
		counts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to delete", deletes))
	}
	if replacements > 0 {
		counts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to replace", replacements))
	}

	if len(counts) == 0 {
		return "Plan: No changes."
	}

	// Join counts with commas when multiple
	if len(counts) == 1 {
		return fmt.Sprintf("Plan: %s.", counts[0])
	}

	countStr := ""
	for i, count := range counts {
		if i > 0 && i == len(counts)-1 {
			countStr += ", " + count
		} else if i > 0 {
			countStr += ", " + count
		} else {
			countStr = count
		}
	}

	return fmt.Sprintf("Plan: %s.", countStr)
}

// summarizeCounts returns a summary line with counts of each action type
func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) summarizeCounts(groups map[plans.Action][]string) string {
	creates := len(groups[plans.Create])
	updates := len(groups[plans.Update])
	deletes := len(groups[plans.Delete])
	replacements := len(groups[plans.DeleteThenCreate]) + len(groups[plans.CreateThenDelete])

	var counts []string
	if creates > 0 {
		counts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to create", creates))
	}
	if updates > 0 {
		counts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to update", updates))
	}
	if deletes > 0 {
		counts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to delete", deletes))
	}
	if replacements > 0 {
		counts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to replace", replacements))
	}

	if len(counts) == 0 {
		return "Plan: No changes."
	}

	// Join counts with commas when multiple
	if len(counts) == 1 {
		return fmt.Sprintf("Plan: %s.", counts[0])
	}

	countStr := ""
	for i, count := range counts {
		if i > 0 && i == len(counts)-1 {
			countStr += ", " + count
		} else if i > 0 {
			countStr += ", " + count
		} else {
			countStr = count
		}
	}

	return fmt.Sprintf("Plan: %s.", countStr)
}
After
// summarizeCounts returns a summary line with counts of each action type
func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) summarizeCounts(groups map[plans.Action][]string) string {
	creates := len(groups[plans.Create])
	updates := len(groups[plans.Update])
	deletes := len(groups[plans.Delete])
	replacements := len(groups[plans.DeleteThenCreate]) + len(groups[plans.CreateThenDelete])

	var counts []string
	if creates > 0 {
		counts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to create", creates))
	}
	if updates > 0 {
		counts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to update", updates))
	}
	if deletes > 0 {
		counts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to delete", deletes))
	}
	if replacements > 0 {
		counts = append(counts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to replace", replacements))
	}

	if len(counts) == 0 {
		return "Plan: No changes."
	}

	// Join counts with commas
	var countStr string
	for i, count := range counts {
		if i == 0 {
			countStr = count
		} else {
			countStr += ", " + count
		}
	}

	return fmt.Sprintf("Plan: %s.", countStr)
}

	// Collect all resource changes
